					if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDrugs] > 1000 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pUpdate] < 2) SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "Вы не можете взять столько наркотиков.");
					if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDrugs] > 1000 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pUpdate] < 2) return PlayerInfo[playerid][pDrugs] -= strval(inputtext);

					SaveStoreRifa();
				}
